- `fascinated/captivated by online booking and high-level hotel services offered by hotels`

**식당 핵심 변환**
- `franchise restaurants and private restaurants`
- `dining services to restaurant users`
- 동사: `go → frequent / patronize` ("patronize는 동사로 격상")
- `large number of people frequent restaurants for various purposes` / `patronized restaurants`
- `to enjoy meals or dine in`
- `using the applications instead of physically visiting restaurants in person`
- 시설 칭찬: `there is a CCTV camera so that we can have more safety` / `the staff are very kind and friendly, welcoming, ready to serve` / `well maintained, clean and comfortable`

##### E. 자료 #11 → spec 컬럼 매핑

| 컬럼 | 적재 후보 |
|------|---------|
| `evaluation_criteria` | 4대 AL 기준(Vocab/Agreement/Preposition/Syntax) 흠 판정 룰 + Cohesive devices |
| `coaching_focus` | "첫 문제가 가장 중요" → 첫 문장 Skeleton paragraph + Breath of Vocabulary 우선 |
| `model_answer_spec` | 만능 패턴 7 Step 구조 |
| `example_model_answer` | 은행/호텔/식당 풀 모범 3종 |
| `tone_adjustment` | Step 0 시간 벌기 — IH·AL 학생 모두 권장. 자연스러움 보완 도구 |

#### [원자료 #12] 9강. AL 적용 심사 기준 #5 — Cohesive devices (환경 주제 적용 — `11.txt`) — 2026-05-16 수신

##### A. 강사 핵심 메시지

| 메시지 | 함의 |
|--------|------|
| "Connect words and phrases and cohesive devices를 돌발 주제에 비교에 공부해 보자" | 평가 기준 + 적용 동시 학습 |
| "한 문장으로 이야기 X, 두 개를 묶어서 이야기" | **문장 단위 → 단락 단위** 발화 능력 — ACTFL paragraph-level discourse 기준 |
| "Cohesive devices 자체가 굉장히 중요한 요소" | 단순 표현 격상이 아니라 **단락 결속력** 측정 |
| "IH 채점하는 곳에 reparative 표시가 많이 되어 있다" | IH 학생은 cohesive device 반복 사용 → 흠 체크됨 |
| "어드밴스는 적극적으로 사용해야 한다" | AL 학생은 6 카테고리에서 골고루 동원해야 |

##### B. 재활용 풀 모범 (영어 인용)

```
It's a tough question. I haven't thought about it. I don't know what to say. What am I supposed to say? But I'll do my best.

Generally speaking, it is often said that these days environmental issues are emerging. One of them would be recycling. If I had to choose one, it would be recycling.

There is no doubt that we take it very seriously. We take it very seriously without a doubt. It is unquably true that we take it very seriously.

To talk about recycling, first of all, generally speaking, we recycle regularly on a regular basis. Therefore, leading to the fact that we have a sophisticated recycling system / highly advanced recycling system for materials like plastic and aluminum and glass.

As long as I know, the government has strict rules on recycling. If you don't do it, you get fined.

Besides, a lot of foreign people come to Korea. They are fascinated by our well-practiced recycling. I'm so proud of being Korean.

In conclusion, I think we are performing well based on the trend so far. We hope to continue improving in the future. I hope this trend continues just like this forever.
```

##### C. 환경 마무리 멘트(토론적 결론 — AL 격상 결정적)

> 강사 명시: "이 내용은 리스닝 다 카페에서 한 외국인 학생이 한 내용을 약간 변형해서 제가 마음에 들어 드린 겁니다." — **AL 학생용 마무리 카드**

```
The planet we are living on is not ours. It belongs to our children's children.
So we should pass it on to the next generation as it is now.
This is not an option. This is a must.
By doing this, we can make the better world. We can make better Korea.
```

##### D. 지리(지형) 풀 모범

```
It is a tough question. I haven't thought about it.
Speaking of geography here in Korea, we have numerous mountains, rivers, and lakes.

The first thing is that Korea is situated on the Korean peninsula, surrounded by the sea on three sides, leading to the fact that we have thousands of islands along the coast.

In addition / On top of that, we are blessed with abundant seafood and marine resources, with 70% of our territory being mountainous.

For instance, the tallest mountain is Baekdusan and the second tallest one is [Mt. ...].

It is undoubtedly true that some areas are recognized by UNESCO. Therefore, when foreign people come to Korea, they are so fascinated and captivated by the beautiful nature of Korea.

[+ 환경 마무리 토론 멘트 연결]
```

##### E. 지구온난화 풀 모범

```
It is important to note that the earth is gradually warming.
For instance / for example / to give you some details, global temperature is steadily increasing, leading to the melting of icebergs and glaciers.

On top of that, sea levels are rising, causing changes in coastal areas. The habitat of polar bears and penguins is decreasing. The ecosystem is heavily influenced by that.

In addition / additionally, this phenomenon is known as global warming.

To slow down global warming, we do recycling. The Korean government has strict rules on that. So if you don't do it, you get fined. We are performing well on recycling regardless of age or gender based on the trend so far.

[+ 환경 마무리 토론 멘트 연결]
```

##### F. 날씨·계절 풀 모범

```
Tough question. I haven't thought about it.
To talk about the weather and the seasons in Korea, generally speaking, we experience four distinct seasons: spring, summer, fall, and winter.

For instance, in spring, the weather is nice and mild. It is moderately warm without being too hot or too cold.

On the other hand, summer is hot and humid with scorching temperatures that can feel burning hot. It is sticky hot.

In addition, fall is considered a nice time of the year. A large number of people go hiking to see the fallen leaves turning colorful.

Besides, winter, however, is freezing cold and dry. A large portion of the population enjoy skiing and snowboarding.

One thing that I'd like to talk about is global warming. Because of global warming, the global temperature goes up every year, leading to the fact that glaciers and icebergs are melting, which causes habitat decrease of polar bears and penguins in the north.
```

##### G. 자료 #12 → spec 컬럼 매핑

| 컬럼 | 적재 후보 |
|------|---------|
| `evaluation_criteria` | Cohesive devices 6 카테고리 다양성 측정 룰 + "repetitive" 흠 판정 |
| `coaching_focus` | "두 문장을 묶어 이야기" — 단락 결속력. 6 카테고리 골고루 동원 |
| `example_model_answer` | 재활용/지리/지구온난화/날씨 풀 모범 4종 + 환경 토론 마무리 |
| `tone_adjustment` | 환경은 토론적 결론이 AL 격상 핵심 — "the planet belongs to children's children" 카드 |

#### [원자료 #13] 9강. AL 적용 심사 기준 — Breath of Vocabulary 심화 (산업·기술 주제 적용 — `12.txt`) — 2026-05-16 수신

##### A. 강사 핵심 메시지

| 메시지 | 함의 |
|--------|------|
| "산업과 기술은 다르지 않다" | **산업 = 기술 같은 패턴 답변** — 강사 명시 |
| "이 다 둘 다 가지로 풀 수 있다 하나의 군 즉 어떤 공동체로 보세요" | 출제 시 분류 X — 같은 답변 사용 |
| "AL은 어휘 폭이 결정적" | Breath of Vocabulary가 산업·기술 핵심 측정축 |

##### B. 한국 산업·기술 종류(강사 열거)

`IT industry` / `food industry` / `secondary battery industry` / `automobile industry` / `petrol chemical industry` / `pharmaceutical industry` + 기술: `semiconductor` / `smartphone` / `metaverse` / `cloud computing` / `AI` + 문화: `K-pop` / `BTS` / `new jeans` / `Korean wave`

##### C. 핵심 어휘 격상 매트릭스 (자료 #13 풀 — Breath of Vocabulary 적용)

| 일반 어휘 (IH) | AL 격상 후보 (강사 명시) |
|----------|---------|
| many | numerous · countless · thousands of · millions of · a large number of · a great deal of · a substantial number of · a large portion of |
| good | high-level · sophisticated · highly advanced · superior |
| famous · popular | gain fame · on the rise · booming · getting more attention from the public · become trendy and sensational |
| foreign people | numerous international visitors |
| amazed | captivated · fascinated · stunned |
| best features | unparalleled excellence and characteristics |
| I'm so proud | It fills me with an immense sense of pride · I (definitely) have a strong sense of pride |
| 시장 점유율 | "whose market share is more than 30% globally, which is truly dominant / tremendous" · "It can be said to be superior" |

##### D. 산업·기술 풀 모범 (자료 #13 영어 인용)

```
It's a tough question. I haven't thought about it. I don't have much to talk about, but I'll do my best.

There are numerous kinds of industries here in Korea such as IT industry, food industry, secondary battery industry, automobile industry, petrol chemical industry, pharmaceutical industry, among others.

If I had to choose one, it would be the smartphone industry / semiconductor industry. It would be the smartphone technology.

[정량화] Samsung Electronics has gained fame all around the world, whose market share is more than 30% globally, which is truly dominant.

[인기 격상] Metaverse is on the rise. Metaverse is booming. Cloud computing services are on the rise. It is getting more attention from the public. AI has become trendy and sensational.

[+ K-pop/BTS/한류] Korean wave has gained fame all around the world. K-pop is booming. New Jeans is on the rise. K-pop is truly getting more attention from the public all around the world. It has become trendy and sensational.

Numerous international visitors come to Korea. They are captivated by its unparalleled excellence and characteristics. I'm so proud of that as a Korean. It fills me with an immense sense of pride.

In conclusion, I think we are performing well based on the trend so far. I hope we continue to improve in the foreseeable future. I hope this trend continues just like this forever. We can keep it up.
```

##### E. 자료 #13 → spec 컬럼 매핑

| 컬럼 | 적재 후보 |
|------|---------|
| `evaluation_criteria` | Breath of Vocabulary 폭 측정 — `many/good/famous/people/amazed` 반복 → 흠 |
| `coaching_focus` | "내가 못 쓰는 표현 한두 개 박아 넣기" — 전부 어려운 어휘 X. 자연스러움 + 일부 격상 |
| `example_model_answer` | 산업·기술 풀 모범 (반도체/스마트폰) + K-pop/BTS 변환 패턴 |
| `coaching_system` 본문 | "산업 = 기술 같은 패턴" — 학생 부담 경감 메시지 |

#### [원자료 #14] 10강. AL 적용 심사 기준 마무리 — 개인 돌발 (`13.txt`) — 2026-05-16 수신

##### A. 강사 핵심 메시지

| 메시지 | 함의 |
|--------|------|
| "개인 돌발은 돌발 주제 중 가장 쉬운 문제로 간주" | 학생 부담 ↓ — 누구나 겪는 개인 문제 |
| "오답을 잘 못 하면 좌절이 더 크다" | **반대로 못 하면 등급 충격 大** — 주의 |
| "Vocabulary의 폭을 넓히는 동시에 기존의 배운 내용들을 돌발 주제에 사용하는 연습" | 마무리 강의 — 누적 적용 |

##### B. 개인 돌발 2대 출제 토픽 (강사 명시)

| 토픽 | DB 매핑 | 답변 전략 |
|------|---------|---------|
| **휴일/celebration/gathering** (서로 호환) | `일반·휴일` / `일반·모임` | 추석(Chuseok) → "Korean Thanksgiving" 등치 / family bonding |
| **자유시간** (free time) | `일반·자유시간` | **100% 스마트폰 답변 → 최고의 만능** |

##### C. 추석 풀 모범 (영어 인용 자료 #14)

```
It's a tough question. I don't know what to say, but I'll do my best.

Generally speaking, there are numerous types of holidays celebrated here in Korea, such as New Year's Day and Chuseok, which is Thanksgiving as well around the world.

It is often said that one of the major Korean holidays is definitely Chuseok. Chuseok is a day of thanksgiving in Korea when families gather together / get together / come together to spend time with each other.

During this holiday, various activities take place. For instance, families set up special meals and often wear traditional clothing.

Furthermore, an important tradition during Chuseok is the ancestral ritual to honor their ancestors. People also make a special rice cake called Songpyeon.

In addition / on top of that / besides, Chuseok is considered valuable time for family harmony and gratitude.

In conclusion / the bottom line is that I've been very busy these days, so I hope I can spend more precious time with my family.

Family is my whole world. Family comes first like always. I put my family as a priority in my life. Some people say celebrating holidays is for relaxation, but to me it is a family bonding time.

When foreign people come to Korea, they are so fascinated by the Korean culture and the background of Korean traditions.
```

##### D. 자유시간(스마트폰) 풀 모범 — 양면 토론 구조 (AL 격상 핵심)

> 강사: "자유시간 답변은 100% 스마트폰. 좋은 점·나쁜 점 → 해결책 → 토론적 결론 = AL 격상 골격." 양면 토론 구조로 ACTFL "discussion" 측정 충족.

```
[Step 1 — 일반화] It is often said that these days I've been incredibly busy / extremely busy / significantly busy, especially on weekdays. Therefore, I've had limited free time, leading to the fact that I've had limited free time. However, I do have a lot of free time on weekends or holidays.

[Step 2 — 좋은 점] Generally speaking, most of the time I use smartphones for entertainment / for entertaining purposes. It is a good source for videos that I'm interested in. Sometimes crying, sometimes laughing.

The best part is that it is absolutely free. It doesn't cost anything. I can dive deep into many favorite subjects and have unlimited access to my interests.

[Step 3 — 반전 → 나쁜 점] On the other hand, the bad thing is that I become someone addicted to it. The drawback is that when I don't watch YouTube or don't have my smartphone with me, I get this strange feeling like something is missing in my life.

[Step 4 — 해결책] Therefore / on top of that / leading to the fact that, I realized I need to cut back on this addiction and find the solution soon. It is imperative to cut back on the usage of a smartphone. I'd like to allocate my quality time with my family.

[Step 5 — 토론적 결론 (AL 격상 결정적)]
Technology is supposed to make people's lives convenient. It is one thing, but the other thing is that it makes us unable to sustain the healthy relationship with others — which is a big shame. Technological development is supposed to bring people closer, but ironically, it makes us further apart.
```

##### E. 자료 #14 → spec 컬럼 매핑

| 컬럼 | 적재 후보 |
|------|---------|
| `evaluation_criteria` | 누적 적용 — 4대 AL 기준 + Cohesive + Breath of Vocabulary 종합 측정 |
| `coaching_focus` | 자유시간 = 100% 스마트폰 / 양면 토론 구조(좋은 점 → 반전 → 나쁜 점 → 해결책 → 토론적 결론) |
| `example_model_answer` | 추석 풀 모범 + 자유시간 스마트폰 풀 모범 |
| `tone_adjustment` | 개인 돌발은 부담 ↓ 메시지 — "다행이다 / 할 말이 있다" 격려 |

#### 돌발 코칭 spec → 30 질문 화이트리스트 + **4 그룹 분기** (구현 결정 — 사용자 확정 2026-05-16)

**돌발은 question_type이 아니다. 30 질문 화이트리스트 + 코칭 진입 시 4 그룹별 spec 자동 선택.**

##### 🚨 사용자 확정 — 단일 spec X, **4 그룹 분기**

> 자료 #11~#14는 4 그룹마다 코칭 요소가 명확히 다름. 단일 description_random spec X. **4 row 분기 spec**.

| spec ID | 적용 토픽 | DB 질문 수 | 코칭 핵심 요소 (자료 #11~#14에서 추출) |
|--------|---------|---------|---------|
| **`description_random_current_affairs`** (시사) | 은행·호텔·음식점·교통 | 8 | 자료 #11 — 4대 AL 기준(Vocab/Agreement/Preposition/Syntax) + 어휘 격상 매트릭스(`numerous/spot/refer to/for various purposes/large portion of population`) + 시사 토픽 풀 모범 3종(은행·호텔·식당) + 디지털 대체(`online booking/mobile banking instead of physically visiting in person`) |
| **`description_random_environment`** (환경) | 재활용·지형·날씨 | 8 | 자료 #12 — **Cohesive devices 6 카테고리 강조**(repetitive 흠 회피) + 환경 4 토픽 풀 모범(재활용/지리/지구온난화/날씨) + **토론적 마무리 멘트**("the planet belongs to children's children · This is not an option, this is a must") AL 격상 결정 |
| **`description_random_industry_tech`** (산업·기술) | 산업·기술 | 8 | 자료 #13 — **Breath of Vocabulary 심화** + 어휘 격상 매트릭스 8 카테고리(`gain fame/booming/captivated/unparalleled excellence/immense sense of pride`) + **시장 점유율 정량화**(`more than 30% globally, which is truly dominant`) + 외국인 반응 자랑 강화 |
| **`description_random_personal`** (개인) | 모임·휴일·자유시간 | 6 | 자료 #14 — **양면 토론 구조**(좋은 점 → 반전 → 나쁜 점 → 해결책 → 토론적 결론) AL 격상 결정 + 가족 emphasis(`family is my whole world / family bonding time`) + 추석 풀 모범 + 자유시간 = 100% 스마트폰 답변 |

##### 4 그룹 모두 공유하는 공통 base

> 4 row 모두 아래 공통 요소 포함 — `coaching_system` 본문에 한 번만 정의하고 4 row가 참조:

- 만능 패턴 7 Step (Step 0 시간 벌기 → 1 일반화 → 2 종류 분류 → 3 사용자·이용 → 4 트렌드 반전 → 5 외국인 반응 → 6 본인 자랑 → 7 결론·전망)
- 4대 AL 기준(Vocabulary breadth / Agreement / Preposition / Syntax)
- Cohesive devices 6 카테고리 다양화
- 사용자 친화 포맷팅("못 쓰는 표현 한두 개 박아 넣기")
- 페르소나 톤(부담 경감)

##### 구현 분기 룰

| 결정 항목 | 판단 |
|---------|------|
| `QUESTION_TYPES` 상수 추가? | **X** — 기존 10유형 유지 |
| 4축 매칭 (1차 필터) | `survey_type='공통형' AND category='일반' AND topic IN [13 토픽] AND question_type='description'` → 30 질문 식별 |
| 5축 분기 (2차 — 4 그룹) | `topic`에 따라 4 그룹 분류: **시사**(은행/호텔/음식점/교통) / **환경**(재활용/지형/날씨) / **산업·기술**(산업/기술) / **개인**(모임/휴일/자유시간) |
| EF 진입 시 spec 선택 | 4축 매칭 일치 + topic으로 그룹 결정 → 4 그룹 중 하나의 spec 자동 선택 |
| 매칭 불일치 시 | 해당 `question_type`의 일반 spec 적용 (routine/comparison/past_*/adv_*/rp_*) |
| 학생 배경 서베이 선택 여부 | **무관** (사용자 확정 2026-05-16) |
| 코칭 진입 UX | 학생에게 "돌발 / 시사 / 환경 / 산업·기술 / 개인" 그룹 노출 X — 시스템 내부 자동 분기, 학생은 코칭 결과만 받음 |
| `coaching_specs` 행 수 (`description` 계열) | **5 row** — 일반 description (선택형 묘사 — 자료 #1+#5 기반) **+** description_random × 4 그룹 (시사/환경/산업·기술/개인) |
| 부정확한 매칭 위험 | 같은 토픽(예: 은행)이라도 `past_special`("Sometimes problems arise with the bank...") 질문에 만능 패턴 적용 시 부적합 — 사건 회상 골격 필요. **4축 매칭 엄격 적용 필수** |

#### 분류 결과 (3축) — 자료 #11~#14 종합

| 축 | 분류 |
|---|------|
| 공통 vs 유형 | **공통** (4대 AL 기준 + Cohesive devices + 만능 패턴 = 모든 돌발 답변 골격) + **유형별 토픽 모범**(은행·호텔·식당·재활용·지리·지구온난화·날씨·산업·기술·휴일·자유시간 11종) |
| 등급 | **IH·AL 둘 다** — IH에서 시작해 AL로 격상하는 과정 전체 (자료 #11·#12·#13이 격상 매트릭스 직접 제공) |
| spec 컬럼 | `evaluation_criteria`(4대 AL + Cohesive 흠 룰) / `coaching_focus`(만능 패턴 7 Step + 어휘 격상 매트릭스) / `model_answer_spec`(7 Step 구조) / `example_model_answer`(11 토픽 풀 모범) / `tone_adjustment`(부담 경감 페르소나) / `coaching_system` 본문(돌발 정의·4그룹·산업=기술 메시지) |
| 평가엔진 정합 | `ADV-2-V*`(Vocabulary breadth) / `ADV-2-G1~3`(Agreement·Preposition·Syntax) / `ADV-2-CD1~3`(Cohesive devices) — **소리담 평가엔진 4대 AL 기준과 강사 4대 기준이 완전히 일치** (자료 #5의 12번 q12_gatekeeper에 이어 두 번째 검증된 정합) |
| 자료 #5(Skeleton)와의 관계 | 자료 #5는 Skeleton paragraph 도구를 제공(IH→AL 진입 골격), 자료 #11~#14는 그 도구를 돌발 4그룹·11 토픽에 직접 적용한 실전 매트릭스. **상호 보완. 돌발 spec 완성형.** |
